Comment Key: ClinicalExamComment
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Leukocytes in urine, no blood, no nitrates and no UTI symptoms

Ways to reduce inflammation include a mediterranean style diet, avoiding sugar and trans fats, exercise, not smoking, avoiding toxins as much as possible, maintaining an ideal body weight and stress reduction.
